public static byte[] toBigEndianUtf16Bytes(char[] chars, int offset, int length){byte[] result = new byte[length * 2];int end = offset + length;int resultIndex = 0;for (int i = offset; i < end; ++i){char ch = chars[i];result[resultIndex++] = (byte)((ch >>> 8)); // big endian shiftresult[resultIndex++] = (byte)ch;}return result;}Note: In java, the bit shift operator ">>" is an arithmetic shift operator while ">>>â€ is a logical shift operator.
